// ============================================================================
// --- POOL FINDER MODULE (PRODUCTION-READY) ---
// ============================================================================

/// DEX type enumeration for pool identification
#[derive(Debug, Clone, PartialEq, Eq, Hash)]
pub enum DexType {
    RaydiumAmmV4,
    RaydiumClmm,
    RaydiumCpmm,
    OrcaWhirlpool,
    MeteoraDlmm,
    MeteoraDammV2,
    MeteoraDbc,
    PumpSwap,
    PumpFun,
    Unknown,
}

impl DexType {
    /// Get the program ID for this DEX type
    pub fn program_id(&self) -> &'static str {
        match self {
            DexType::RaydiumAmmV4 => dex_programs::RAYDIUM_AMM_V4_PROGRAM,
            DexType::RaydiumClmm => dex_programs::RAYDIUM_CLMM_PROGRAM,
            DexType::RaydiumCpmm => dex_programs::RAYDIUM_CPMM_PROGRAM,
            DexType::OrcaWhirlpool => dex_programs::ORCA_WHIRLPOOL_PROGRAM,
            DexType::MeteoraDlmm => dex_programs::METEORA_DLMM_PROGRAM,
            DexType::MeteoraDammV2 => dex_programs::METEORA_DAMM_V2_PROGRAM,
            DexType::MeteoraDbc => dex_programs::METEORA_DBC_PROGRAM,
            DexType::PumpSwap => dex_programs::PUMPSWAP_PROGRAM,
            DexType::PumpFun => dex_programs::PUMPFUN_PROGRAM,
            DexType::Unknown => "",
        }
    }

    /// Get a human-readable name for this DEX type
    pub fn display_name(&self) -> &'static str {
        match self {
            DexType::RaydiumAmmV4 => "Raydium AMM V4",
            DexType::RaydiumClmm => "Raydium CLMM",
            DexType::RaydiumCpmm => "Raydium CPMM",
            DexType::OrcaWhirlpool => "Orca Whirlpool",
            DexType::MeteoraDlmm => "Meteora DLMM",
            DexType::MeteoraDammV2 => "Meteora DAMM V2",
            DexType::MeteoraDbc => "Meteora DBC",
            DexType::PumpSwap => "PumpSwap",
            DexType::PumpFun => "Pump.fun",
            DexType::Unknown => "Unknown",
        }
    }

    /// Create DexType from program ID string
    pub fn from_program_id(program_id: &str) -> Self {
        match program_id {
            id if id == dex_programs::RAYDIUM_AMM_V4_PROGRAM => DexType::RaydiumAmmV4,
            id if id == dex_programs::RAYDIUM_CLMM_PROGRAM => DexType::RaydiumClmm,
            id if id == dex_programs::RAYDIUM_CPMM_PROGRAM => DexType::RaydiumCpmm,
            id if id == dex_programs::ORCA_WHIRLPOOL_PROGRAM => DexType::OrcaWhirlpool,
            id if id == dex_programs::METEORA_DLMM_PROGRAM => DexType::MeteoraDlmm,
            id if id == dex_programs::METEORA_DAMM_V2_PROGRAM => DexType::MeteoraDammV2,
            id if id == dex_programs::METEORA_DBC_PROGRAM => DexType::MeteoraDbc,
            id if id == dex_programs::PUMPSWAP_PROGRAM => DexType::PumpSwap,
            id if id == dex_programs::PUMPFUN_PROGRAM => DexType::PumpFun,
            _ => DexType::Unknown,
        }
    }

    /// Create DexType from DEX name string (for DexScreener integration)
    pub fn from_dex_name(name: &str) -> Self {
        let name_lower = name.to_lowercase();
        if name_lower.contains("raydium") && name_lower.contains("clmm") {
            DexType::RaydiumClmm
        } else if name_lower.contains("raydium") && name_lower.contains("cpmm") {
            DexType::RaydiumCpmm
        } else if name_lower.contains("raydium") {
            DexType::RaydiumAmmV4
        } else if name_lower.contains("orca") || name_lower.contains("whirlpool") {
            DexType::OrcaWhirlpool
        } else if name_lower.contains("meteora") && name_lower.contains("dlmm") {
            DexType::MeteoraDlmm
        } else if name_lower.contains("meteora") && name_lower.contains("dbc") {
            DexType::MeteoraDbc
        } else if name_lower.contains("meteora") {
            DexType::MeteoraDammV2
        } else if name_lower.contains("pumpswap") {
            DexType::PumpSwap
        } else if name_lower.contains("pump") {
            DexType::PumpFun
        } else {
            DexType::Unknown
        }
    }
}

impl std::fmt::Display for DexType {
    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
        write!(f, "{}", self.display_name())
    }
}

/// Enhanced discovered pool with full metadata for validation
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct ValidatedPool {
    /// Pool address on-chain
    pub address: String,
    /// DEX type enum
    pub dex_type: DexType,
    /// Human-readable DEX name
    pub dex_name: String,
    /// Token A mint address
    pub token_a_mint: String,
    /// Token B mint address
    pub token_b_mint: String,
    /// Token A symbol (if known)
    pub token_a_symbol: String,
    /// Token B symbol (if known)
    pub token_b_symbol: String,
    /// Token A reserves (raw amount)
    pub reserve_a: u64,
    /// Token B reserves (raw amount)
    pub reserve_b: u64,
    /// Estimated liquidity in USD
    pub liquidity_usd: f64,
    /// Whether pool appears active (recent trades)
    pub is_active: bool,
    /// Quality score (0.0 - 1.0)
    pub quality_score: f64,
    /// Last time pool was validated/updated (unix timestamp)
    pub last_validated: u64,
    /// Number of consecutive parsing failures
    pub consecutive_failures: u32,
    /// Reason for last failure (if any)
    pub last_failure_reason: Option<String>,
}

impl ValidatedPool {
    /// Create a new ValidatedPool with basic info
    pub fn new(address: &str, dex_type: DexType, token_a: &str, token_b: &str) -> Self {
        Self {
            address: address.to_string(),
            dex_name: dex_type.display_name().to_string(),
            dex_type,
            token_a_mint: token_a.to_string(),
            token_b_mint: token_b.to_string(),
            token_a_symbol: String::new(),
            token_b_symbol: String::new(),
            reserve_a: 0,
            reserve_b: 0,
            liquidity_usd: 0.0,
            is_active: false,
            quality_score: 0.0,
            last_validated: 0,
            consecutive_failures: 0,
            last_failure_reason: None,
        }
    }

    /// Check if pool should be considered for subscription
    pub fn is_valid_for_subscription(&self) -> bool {
        self.is_active 
            && self.reserve_a > 0 
            && self.reserve_b > 0 
            && self.consecutive_failures < 3
            && self.quality_score > 0.1
    }

    /// Convert to subscription tuple format for WebSocket manager
    pub fn to_subscription_tuple(&self) -> (String, String) {
        (self.dex_name.clone(), self.address.clone())
    }
}

/// Blacklist entry with reason and timestamp
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct BlacklistEntry {
    pub pool_address: String,
    pub reason: String,
    pub added_at: u64,
    pub auto_added: bool,
}

/// Pool validation thresholds
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct PoolValidationConfig {
    /// Minimum reserve threshold (in smallest unit)
    pub min_reserve_threshold: u64,
    /// Minimum liquidity in USD
    pub min_liquidity_usd: f64,
    /// Maximum consecutive failures before auto-blacklist
    pub max_consecutive_failures: u32,
    /// Maximum price deviation from reference (percentage)
    pub max_price_deviation_percent: f64,
    /// Minimum quality score to be considered valid
    pub min_quality_score: f64,
}

impl Default for PoolValidationConfig {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            min_reserve_threshold: 1_000_000, // 0.001 SOL or 0.001 USDC minimum
            min_liquidity_usd: 10_000.0,      // $10,000 minimum
            max_consecutive_failures: 3,
            max_price_deviation_percent: 50.0, // 50% max deviation from reference
            min_quality_score: 0.1,
        }
    }
}

/// Main Pool Finder struct for discovering and validating pools
pub struct PoolFinder {
    /// Async RPC client
    rpc: Arc<AsyncRpcClient>,
    /// Blacklisted pool addresses
    blacklist: HashSet<String>,
    /// Blacklist entries with metadata
    blacklist_entries: Vec<BlacklistEntry>,
    /// Validation configuration
    config: PoolValidationConfig,
    /// Known problematic pools (hardcoded)
    known_bad_pools: HashSet<String>,
}

impl PoolFinder {
    /// Create a new PoolFinder with default configuration
    pub fn new(rpc: Arc<AsyncRpcClient>) -> Self {
        let mut known_bad_pools = HashSet::new();
        // Add known problematic pools from the problem statement
        known_bad_pools.insert("58oQChx4yWmvKdwLLZzBi4ChoCc2fqCUWBkwMihLYQo2".to_string()); // Zero reserves, wrong parser
        
        Self {
            rpc,
            blacklist: HashSet::new(),
            blacklist_entries: Vec::new(),
            config: PoolValidationConfig::default(),
            known_bad_pools,
        }
    }

    /// Create PoolFinder with custom configuration
    pub fn with_config(rpc: Arc<AsyncRpcClient>, config: PoolValidationConfig) -> Self {
        let mut finder = Self::new(rpc);
        finder.config = config;
        finder
    }

    /// Add a pool to the blacklist
    pub fn blacklist_pool(&mut self, address: &str, reason: &str) {
        if !self.blacklist.contains(address) {
            self.blacklist.insert(address.to_string());
            self.blacklist_entries.push(BlacklistEntry {
                pool_address: address.to_string(),
                reason: reason.to_string(),
                added_at: std::time::SystemTime::now()
                    .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)
                    .unwrap_or_default()
                    .as_secs(),
                auto_added: false,
            });
            println!("[PoolFinder] Blacklisted pool: {} - {}", address, reason);
        }
    }

    /// Auto-blacklist a pool due to repeated failures
    fn auto_blacklist_pool(&mut self, address: &str, reason: &str) {
        if !self.blacklist.contains(address) {
            self.blacklist.insert(address.to_string());
            self.blacklist_entries.push(BlacklistEntry {
                pool_address: address.to_string(),
                reason: format!("Auto-blacklisted: {}", reason),
                added_at: std::time::SystemTime::now()
                    .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)
                    .unwrap_or_default()
                    .as_secs(),
                auto_added: true,
            });
            println!("[PoolFinder] Auto-blacklisted pool: {} - {}", address, reason);
        }
    }

    /// Remove a pool from the blacklist
    pub fn unblacklist_pool(&mut self, address: &str) {
        self.blacklist.remove(address);
        self.blacklist_entries.retain(|e| e.pool_address != address);
        println!("[PoolFinder] Removed {} from blacklist", address);
    }

    /// Check if a pool is blacklisted
    pub fn is_blacklisted(&self, address: &str) -> bool {
        self.blacklist.contains(address) || self.known_bad_pools.contains(address)
    }

    /// Get blacklist entries
    pub fn get_blacklist(&self) -> &[BlacklistEntry] {
        &self.blacklist_entries
    }

    /// Validate a single pool's token pair
    pub fn validate_token_pair(
        &self,
        pool: &ValidatedPool,
        expected_token_a: &str,
        expected_token_b: &str,
    ) -> bool {
        // Check both orderings
        let matches_forward = pool.token_a_mint == expected_token_a 
            && pool.token_b_mint == expected_token_b;
        let matches_reverse = pool.token_a_mint == expected_token_b 
            && pool.token_b_mint == expected_token_a;
        
        if !matches_forward && !matches_reverse {
            println!("[PoolFinder] Token pair mismatch for {}: expected {}/{} or {}/{}, got {}/{}",
                pool.address,
                &expected_token_a[..8.min(expected_token_a.len())],
                &expected_token_b[..8.min(expected_token_b.len())],
                &expected_token_b[..8.min(expected_token_b.len())],
                &expected_token_a[..8.min(expected_token_a.len())],
                &pool.token_a_mint[..8.min(pool.token_a_mint.len())],
                &pool.token_b_mint[..8.min(pool.token_b_mint.len())],
            );
            return false;
        }
        true
    }

    /// Validate pool reserves
    pub fn validate_reserves(&self, pool: &ValidatedPool) -> bool {
        if pool.reserve_a < self.config.min_reserve_threshold {
            println!("[PoolFinder] Reserve A too low for {}: {} < {}",
                pool.address, pool.reserve_a, self.config.min_reserve_threshold);
            return false;
        }
        if pool.reserve_b < self.config.min_reserve_threshold {
            println!("[PoolFinder] Reserve B too low for {}: {} < {}",
                pool.address, pool.reserve_b, self.config.min_reserve_threshold);
            return false;
        }
        true
    }

    /// Validate pool liquidity
    pub fn validate_liquidity(&self, pool: &ValidatedPool) -> bool {
        if pool.liquidity_usd < self.config.min_liquidity_usd {
            println!("[PoolFinder] Liquidity too low for {}: ${:.2} < ${:.2}",
                pool.address, pool.liquidity_usd, self.config.min_liquidity_usd);
            return false;
        }
        true
    }

    /// Calculate quality score for a pool (0.0 - 1.0)
    pub fn calculate_quality_score(&self, pool: &ValidatedPool) -> f64 {
        let mut score = 0.0;
        
        // Liquidity score (0-0.4) - higher liquidity = better
        let liquidity_score = if pool.liquidity_usd > 1_000_000.0 {
            0.4
        } else if pool.liquidity_usd > 100_000.0 {
            0.3
        } else if pool.liquidity_usd > 10_000.0 {
            0.2
        } else {
            0.1
        };
        score += liquidity_score;
        
        // Reserve balance score (0-0.2) - balanced reserves = better
        if pool.reserve_a > 0 && pool.reserve_b > 0 {
            let ratio = pool.reserve_a as f64 / pool.reserve_b as f64;
            // Penalize very unbalanced pools
            if ratio > 0.001 && ratio < 1000.0 {
                score += 0.2;
            } else if ratio > 0.0001 && ratio < 10000.0 {
                score += 0.1;
            }
        }
        
        // Active status score (0-0.2)
        if pool.is_active {
            score += 0.2;
        }
        
        // Failure penalty (0-0.2)
        let failure_penalty = (pool.consecutive_failures as f64 * 0.05).min(0.2);
        score = (score - failure_penalty).max(0.0);
        
        // DEX type bonus (0-0.2) - established DEXs get bonus
        let dex_bonus = match pool.dex_type {
            DexType::RaydiumAmmV4 | DexType::RaydiumClmm => 0.15,
            DexType::OrcaWhirlpool => 0.15,
            DexType::MeteoraDlmm | DexType::MeteoraDammV2 => 0.1,
            _ => 0.05,
        };
        score += dex_bonus;
        
        score.min(1.0)
    }

    /// Validate a pool against all criteria
    pub async fn validate_pool(
        &self,
        pool: &mut ValidatedPool,
        expected_token_a: &str,
        expected_token_b: &str,
    ) -> bool {
        // Check blacklist first
        if self.is_blacklisted(&pool.address) {
            println!("[PoolFinder] Pool {} is blacklisted", pool.address);
            return false;
        }

        // Validate token pair
        if !pool.token_a_mint.is_empty() && !pool.token_b_mint.is_empty() {
            if !self.validate_token_pair(pool, expected_token_a, expected_token_b) {
                pool.last_failure_reason = Some("Token pair mismatch".to_string());
                return false;
            }
        }

        // Validate reserves
        if !self.validate_reserves(pool) {
            pool.last_failure_reason = Some("Insufficient reserves".to_string());
            return false;
        }

        // Validate liquidity
        if !self.validate_liquidity(pool) {
            pool.last_failure_reason = Some("Insufficient liquidity".to_string());
            return false;
        }

        // Calculate quality score
        pool.quality_score = self.calculate_quality_score(pool);
        
        if pool.quality_score < self.config.min_quality_score {
            pool.last_failure_reason = Some(format!("Quality score too low: {:.2}", pool.quality_score));
            return false;
        }

        // Update validation timestamp
        pool.last_validated = std::time::SystemTime::now()
            .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)
            .unwrap_or_default()
            .as_secs();

        pool.is_active = true;
        true
    }

    /// Record a parsing failure for a pool
    pub fn record_failure(&mut self, pool: &mut ValidatedPool, reason: &str) {
        pool.consecutive_failures += 1;
        pool.last_failure_reason = Some(reason.to_string());
        
        if pool.consecutive_failures >= self.config.max_consecutive_failures {
            self.auto_blacklist_pool(&pool.address, reason);
        }
    }

    /// Record a successful parse for a pool
    pub fn record_success(&mut self, pool: &mut ValidatedPool) {
        pool.consecutive_failures = 0;
        pool.last_failure_reason = None;
        pool.is_active = true;
        pool.last_validated = std::time::SystemTime::now()
            .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)
            .unwrap_or_default()
            .as_secs();
    }

    /// Filter pools to only include valid ones
    pub async fn filter_valid_pools(
        &self,
        pools: Vec<ValidatedPool>,
        expected_token_a: &str,
        expected_token_b: &str,
    ) -> Vec<ValidatedPool> {
        let mut valid_pools = Vec::new();
        
        for mut pool in pools {
            if self.validate_pool(&mut pool, expected_token_a, expected_token_b).await {
                valid_pools.push(pool);
            }
        }
        
        // Sort by quality score (descending)
        valid_pools.sort_by(|a, b| {
            b.quality_score.partial_cmp(&a.quality_score).unwrap_or(std::cmp::Ordering::Equal)
        });
        
        valid_pools
    }

    /// Get subscription list from validated pools
    pub fn get_subscription_list(pools: &[ValidatedPool]) -> Vec<(String, String)> {
        pools.iter()
            .filter(|p| p.is_valid_for_subscription())
            .map(|p| p.to_subscription_tuple())
            .collect()
    }

    /// Convert DiscoveredPool to ValidatedPool
    pub fn from_discovered_pool(discovered: &DiscoveredPool) -> ValidatedPool {
        let dex_type = DexType::from_dex_name(&discovered.dex_name);
        ValidatedPool {
            address: discovered.pool_address.clone(),
            dex_type,
            dex_name: discovered.dex_name.clone(),
            token_a_mint: discovered.base_token.clone(),
            token_b_mint: discovered.quote_token.clone(),
            token_a_symbol: String::new(),
            token_b_symbol: String::new(),
            reserve_a: 0,
            reserve_b: 0,
            liquidity_usd: discovered.liquidity_usd,
            is_active: discovered.liquidity_usd > 0.0,
            quality_score: 0.5, // Default score, will be recalculated on validation
            last_validated: 0,
            consecutive_failures: 0,
            last_failure_reason: None,
        }
    }

    /// Find SOL/USDC pools across all supported DEXs using DexScreener
    pub async fn find_sol_usdc_pools(&mut self) -> Result<Vec<ValidatedPool>> {
        self.find_pools_for_pair(SOL_MINT, USDC_MINT).await
    }

    /// Find pools for any token pair using DexScreener
    pub async fn find_pools_for_pair(
        &mut self,
        token_a: &str,
        token_b: &str,
    ) -> Result<Vec<ValidatedPool>> {
        println!("\n[PoolFinder] Discovering pools for {}/{}...", 
            &token_a[..8.min(token_a.len())], 
            &token_b[..8.min(token_b.len())]);

        // Use the existing discover_pools_for_arbitrage function
        let config = PoolDiscoveryConfig {
            max_pools: 20,
            min_liquidity_usd: self.config.min_liquidity_usd,
            only_working_dexs: true,
        };

        let discovered = discover_pools_for_arbitrage(token_a, token_b, config).await?;
        
        println!("[PoolFinder] Found {} pools from DexScreener", discovered.len());

        // Convert to ValidatedPool and filter
        let mut validated_pools: Vec<ValidatedPool> = discovered.iter()
            .map(|d| Self::from_discovered_pool(d))
            .collect();

        // Remove blacklisted pools
        validated_pools.retain(|p| !self.is_blacklisted(&p.address));

        println!("[PoolFinder] {} pools after blacklist filtering", validated_pools.len());

        // Validate each pool
        let valid_pools = self.filter_valid_pools(validated_pools, token_a, token_b).await;

        println!("[PoolFinder] {} pools passed validation", valid_pools.len());

        // Display summary
        if !valid_pools.is_empty() {
            println!("\n[PoolFinder] Valid Pools Summary:");
            println!("  {:<20} {:<12} {:<12} {:<8}", "DEX", "Liquidity", "Quality", "Active");
            println!("  {}", "-".repeat(56));
            for pool in &valid_pools {
                println!("  {:<20} ${:<11.0} {:<12.2} {}",
                    pool.dex_name,
                    pool.liquidity_usd,
                    pool.quality_score,
                    if pool.is_active { "Yes" } else { "No" }
                );
            }
        }

        Ok(valid_pools)
    }

    /// Refresh pool data without full rediscovery
    pub async fn refresh_pools(&mut self, pools: &mut Vec<ValidatedPool>, token_a: &str, token_b: &str) -> Result<()> {
        println!("[PoolFinder] Refreshing {} pools...", pools.len());
        
        for pool in pools.iter_mut() {
            // Skip blacklisted pools
            if self.is_blacklisted(&pool.address) {
                pool.is_active = false;
                continue;
            }

            // Try to fetch and validate pool data
            match self.fetch_pool_data(pool).await {
                Ok(()) => {
                    if self.validate_pool(pool, token_a, token_b).await {
                        self.record_success(pool);
                    }
                }
                Err(e) => {
                    self.record_failure(pool, &e.to_string());
                }
            }
        }

        // Remove pools that exceeded failure threshold
        pools.retain(|p| p.consecutive_failures < self.config.max_consecutive_failures);

        Ok(())
    }

    /// Fetch fresh pool data from RPC
    async fn fetch_pool_data(&self, pool: &mut ValidatedPool) -> Result<()> {
        let pubkey = Pubkey::from_str(&pool.address)
            .context("Invalid pool address")?;

        let account = self.rpc.get_account(&pubkey).await
            .context("Failed to fetch pool account")?;

        // Update pool metadata based on account owner
        let owner = account.owner.to_string();
        pool.dex_type = DexType::from_program_id(&owner);
        
        // For now, just verify the account exists and has data
        if account.data.is_empty() {
            return Err(anyhow!("Pool account has no data"));
        }

        Ok(())
    }

    /// Display blacklist status
    pub fn display_blacklist(&self) {
        if self.blacklist_entries.is_empty() {
            println!("\n[PoolFinder] Blacklist is empty");
            return;
        }

        println!("\n[PoolFinder] Blacklisted Pools ({}):", self.blacklist_entries.len());
        println!("  {:<44} {:<30} {:<6}", "Address", "Reason", "Auto");
        println!("  {}", "-".repeat(84));
        
        for entry in &self.blacklist_entries {
            println!("  {:<44} {:<30} {}",
                &entry.pool_address[..44.min(entry.pool_address.len())],
                &entry.reason[..30.min(entry.reason.len())],
                if entry.auto_added { "Yes" } else { "No" }
            );
        }
    }

    /// Display comprehensive pool validation summary
    pub fn display_validation_summary(pools: &[ValidatedPool]) {
        if pools.is_empty() {
            println!("\n[PoolFinder] No pools to display");
            return;
        }

        println!("\n");
        println!("                    POOL VALIDATION SUMMARY                      ");
        println!("");
        
        let active_count = pools.iter().filter(|p| p.is_active).count();
        let valid_for_sub = pools.iter().filter(|p| p.is_valid_for_subscription()).count();
        let avg_quality: f64 = pools.iter().map(|p| p.quality_score).sum::<f64>() / pools.len() as f64;
        let total_liquidity: f64 = pools.iter().map(|p| p.liquidity_usd).sum();
        
        println!("  Total Pools:        {}", pools.len());
        println!("  Active Pools:       {} ({:.0}%)", active_count, (active_count as f64 / pools.len() as f64) * 100.0);
        println!("  Valid for Sub:      {} ({:.0}%)", valid_for_sub, (valid_for_sub as f64 / pools.len() as f64) * 100.0);
        println!("  Avg Quality Score:  {:.2}", avg_quality);
        println!("  Total Liquidity:    ${:.0}", total_liquidity);
        println!("");
        
        println!("  {:<20} {:<14} {:<10} {:<8} {:<10}", "DEX", "Address", "Liquidity", "Quality", "Status");
        println!("  {}", "-".repeat(66));
        
        for pool in pools.iter().take(15) {
            let status = if pool.is_valid_for_subscription() {
                "Ready"
            } else if pool.is_active {
                "Active"
            } else if pool.consecutive_failures > 0 {
                "Failing"
            } else {
                "Inactive"
            };
            
            println!("  {:<20} {}... ${:<9.0} {:<8.2} {}",
                &pool.dex_name[..20.min(pool.dex_name.len())],
                &pool.address[..10.min(pool.address.len())],
                pool.liquidity_usd,
                pool.quality_score,
                status,
            );
        }
        
        if pools.len() > 15 {
            println!("  ... and {} more pools", pools.len() - 15);
        }
        
        println!("");
    }

    /// Get statistics about pool health
    pub fn get_pool_statistics(pools: &[ValidatedPool]) -> PoolStatistics {
        let total = pools.len();
        let active = pools.iter().filter(|p| p.is_active).count();
        let valid_for_subscription = pools.iter().filter(|p| p.is_valid_for_subscription()).count();
        let with_failures = pools.iter().filter(|p| p.consecutive_failures > 0).count();
        let avg_quality = if total > 0 {
            pools.iter().map(|p| p.quality_score).sum::<f64>() / total as f64
        } else {
            0.0
        };
        let total_liquidity = pools.iter().map(|p| p.liquidity_usd).sum();

        PoolStatistics {
            total_pools: total,
            active_pools: active,
            valid_for_subscription,
            pools_with_failures: with_failures,
            average_quality_score: avg_quality,
            total_liquidity_usd: total_liquidity,
        }
    }
}

/// Statistics about pool health and status
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct PoolStatistics {
    pub total_pools: usize,
    pub active_pools: usize,
    pub valid_for_subscription: usize,
    pub pools_with_failures: usize,
    pub average_quality_score: f64,
    pub total_liquidity_usd: f64,
}

impl std::fmt::Display for PoolStatistics {
    fn fmt(&self, f: &mut std::fmt::Formatter<'_>) -> std::fmt::Result {
        write!(f, "Pools: {}/{} active, {} valid for sub, avg quality: {:.2}, liquidity: ${:.0}",
            self.active_pools,
            self.total_pools,
            self.valid_for_subscription,
            self.average_quality_score,
            self.total_liquidity_usd
        )
    }
}

/// Helper function to integrate PoolFinder with existing Options 3 & 4
pub async fn discover_and_validate_pools(
    rpc: Arc<AsyncRpcClient>,
    token_a: &str,
    token_b: &str,
    min_liquidity: f64,
) -> Result<Vec<(String, String)>> {
    let config = PoolValidationConfig {
        min_liquidity_usd: min_liquidity,
        ..Default::default()
    };
    
    let mut finder = PoolFinder::with_config(rpc, config);
    let pools = finder.find_pools_for_pair(token_a, token_b).await?;
    
    Ok(PoolFinder::get_subscription_list(&pools))
}

// ============================================================================
// --- POOL FINDER UNIT TESTS ---
// ============================================================================

#[cfg(test)]
mod pool_finder_tests {
    use super::*;

    #[test]
    fn test_dex_type_from_program_id() {
        assert_eq!(
            DexType::from_program_id("675kPX9MHTjS2zt1qfr1NYHuzeLXfQM9H24wFSUt1Mp8"),
            DexType::RaydiumAmmV4
        );
        assert_eq!(
            DexType::from_program_id("whirLbMiicVdio4qvUfM5KAg6Ct8VwpYzGff3uctyCc"),
            DexType::OrcaWhirlpool
        );
        assert_eq!(
            DexType::from_program_id("LBUZKhRxPF3XUpBCjp4YzTKgLccjZhTSDM9YuVaPwxo"),
            DexType::MeteoraDlmm
        );
        assert_eq!(
            DexType::from_program_id("unknown_program_id"),
            DexType::Unknown
        );
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_dex_type_from_dex_name() {
        assert_eq!(DexType::from_dex_name("Raydium AMM V4"), DexType::RaydiumAmmV4);
        assert_eq!(DexType::from_dex_name("raydium clmm"), DexType::RaydiumClmm);
        assert_eq!(DexType::from_dex_name("Orca Whirlpool"), DexType::OrcaWhirlpool);
        assert_eq!(DexType::from_dex_name("Meteora DLMM"), DexType::MeteoraDlmm);
        assert_eq!(DexType::from_dex_name("pumpswap"), DexType::PumpSwap);
        assert_eq!(DexType::from_dex_name("some unknown dex"), DexType::Unknown);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_dex_type_display_name() {
        assert_eq!(DexType::RaydiumAmmV4.display_name(), "Raydium AMM V4");
        assert_eq!(DexType::OrcaWhirlpool.display_name(), "Orca Whirlpool");
        assert_eq!(DexType::MeteoraDlmm.display_name(), "Meteora DLMM");
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_validated_pool_new() {
        let pool = ValidatedPool::new(
            "test_address_123",
            DexType::RaydiumAmmV4,
            SOL_MINT,
            USDC_MINT,
        );
        
        assert_eq!(pool.address, "test_address_123");
        assert_eq!(pool.dex_type, DexType::RaydiumAmmV4);
        assert_eq!(pool.token_a_mint, SOL_MINT);
        assert_eq!(pool.token_b_mint, USDC_MINT);
        assert_eq!(pool.reserve_a, 0);
        assert_eq!(pool.reserve_b, 0);
        assert!(!pool.is_active);
        assert_eq!(pool.quality_score, 0.0);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_validated_pool_is_valid_for_subscription() {
        let mut pool = ValidatedPool::new(
            "test_address",
            DexType::RaydiumAmmV4,
            SOL_MINT,
            USDC_MINT,
        );
        
        // Initially not valid (no reserves, not active)
        assert!(!pool.is_valid_for_subscription());
        
        // Set as active with reserves and quality score
        pool.is_active = true;
        pool.reserve_a = 1_000_000_000;
        pool.reserve_b = 100_000_000;
        pool.quality_score = 0.5;
        
        // Now should be valid
        assert!(pool.is_valid_for_subscription());
        
        // Too many failures - not valid
        pool.consecutive_failures = 5;
        assert!(!pool.is_valid_for_subscription());
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_pool_validation_config_default() {
        let config = PoolValidationConfig::default();
        
        assert_eq!(config.min_reserve_threshold, 1_000_000);
        assert_eq!(config.min_liquidity_usd, 10_000.0);
        assert_eq!(config.max_consecutive_failures, 3);
        assert_eq!(config.max_price_deviation_percent, 50.0);
        assert_eq!(config.min_quality_score, 0.1);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_quality_score_calculation() {
        // Create a mock RPC client - we won't actually use it for this test
        let rpc = Arc::new(AsyncRpcClient::new("http://localhost:8899".to_string()));
        let finder = PoolFinder::new(rpc);
        
        // Test low liquidity pool
        let mut pool = ValidatedPool::new("test", DexType::Unknown, SOL_MINT, USDC_MINT);
        pool.liquidity_usd = 5_000.0;
        pool.is_active = false;
        let score = finder.calculate_quality_score(&pool);
        assert!(score < 0.3); // Low score for inactive, low liquidity, unknown DEX
        
        // Test high liquidity active pool on established DEX
        let mut pool2 = ValidatedPool::new("test2", DexType::RaydiumAmmV4, SOL_MINT, USDC_MINT);
        pool2.liquidity_usd = 2_000_000.0;
        pool2.is_active = true;
        pool2.reserve_a = 10_000_000_000;
        pool2.reserve_b = 1_000_000_000;
        let score2 = finder.calculate_quality_score(&pool2);
        assert!(score2 > 0.7); // High score for active, high liquidity, established DEX
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_blacklist_operations() {
        let rpc = Arc::new(AsyncRpcClient::new("http://localhost:8899".to_string()));
        let mut finder = PoolFinder::new(rpc);
        
        // Initially not blacklisted
        assert!(!finder.is_blacklisted("some_pool"));
        
        // Add to blacklist
        finder.blacklist_pool("some_pool", "test reason");
        assert!(finder.is_blacklisted("some_pool"));
        
        // Check blacklist entries
        let entries = finder.get_blacklist();
        assert_eq!(entries.len(), 1);
        assert_eq!(entries[0].pool_address, "some_pool");
        assert_eq!(entries[0].reason, "test reason");
        assert!(!entries[0].auto_added);
        
        // Remove from blacklist
        finder.unblacklist_pool("some_pool");
        assert!(!finder.is_blacklisted("some_pool"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_known_bad_pools_blacklisted() {
        let rpc = Arc::new(AsyncRpcClient::new("http://localhost:8899".to_string()));
        let finder = PoolFinder::new(rpc);
        
        // Known bad pool from problem statement should be blacklisted
        assert!(finder.is_blacklisted("58oQChx4yWmvKdwLLZzBi4ChoCc2fqCUWBkwMihLYQo2"));
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_pool_statistics() {
        let pools = vec![
            {
                let mut p = ValidatedPool::new("p1", DexType::RaydiumAmmV4, SOL_MINT, USDC_MINT);
                p.is_active = true;
                p.reserve_a = 100;
                p.reserve_b = 100;
                p.quality_score = 0.8;
                p.liquidity_usd = 100_000.0;
                p
            },
            {
                let mut p = ValidatedPool::new("p2", DexType::OrcaWhirlpool, SOL_MINT, USDC_MINT);
                p.is_active = true;
                p.reserve_a = 100;
                p.reserve_b = 100;
                p.quality_score = 0.6;
                p.liquidity_usd = 50_000.0;
                p
            },
            {
                let mut p = ValidatedPool::new("p3", DexType::MeteoraDlmm, SOL_MINT, USDC_MINT);
                p.is_active = false;
                p.quality_score = 0.2;
                p.liquidity_usd = 10_000.0;
                p
            },
        ];
        
        let stats = PoolFinder::get_pool_statistics(&pools);
        
        assert_eq!(stats.total_pools, 3);
        assert_eq!(stats.active_pools, 2);
        assert_eq!(stats.valid_for_subscription, 2);
        assert_eq!(stats.pools_with_failures, 0);
        assert!((stats.average_quality_score - 0.533).abs() < 0.01);
        assert_eq!(stats.total_liquidity_usd, 160_000.0);
    }

    #[test]
    fn test_to_subscription_tuple() {
        let pool = ValidatedPool {
            address: "pool_address_123".to_string(),

            dex_name: "Raydium AMM V4".to_string(),

            reserve_b: 1000,
            liquidity_usd: 100_000.0,
            is_active: true,
            quality_score: 0.8,
            last_validated: 0,
            consecutive_failures: 0,
            last_failure_reason: None,
        };
        
        let tuple = pool.to_subscription_tuple();
        assert_eq!(tuple.0, "Raydium AMM V4");
        assert_eq!(tuple.1, "pool_address_123");
    }
}


// ============================================================================
// --- QUOTE FRESHNESS & STALENESS DETECTION ---
// ============================================================================

/// Maximum age for quotes before they're considered stale (milliseconds)
const MAX_QUOTE_AGE_MS: u128 = 2000;  // 2 seconds - aggressive for arbitrage

/// Maximum age for WebSocket price feeds (milliseconds)
const MAX_WS_PRICE_AGE_MS: u128 = 3000;  // 3 seconds for WS feeds

/// Slot-based staleness threshold (Solana-specific)
const MAX_SLOT_STALENESS: u64 = 2;  // Quotes older than 2 slots are stale

/// Quote with full freshness tracking
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct TimestampedQuote {
    pub quote: OrderResponse,
    pub timestamp_ms: u128,
    pub slot: Option<u64>,
    pub dex_name: String,
    pub is_stale: bool,
}

impl TimestampedQuote {
    pub fn new(quote: OrderResponse, dex_name: &str, slot: Option<u64>) -> Self {
        let timestamp_ms = std::time::SystemTime::now()
            .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)
            .unwrap_or_default()
            .as_millis();
        
        Self {
            quote,
            timestamp_ms,
            slot,
            dex_name: dex_name.to_string(),
            is_stale: false,
        }
    }
    
    /// Check if quote has expired based on time
    pub fn is_expired(&self) -> bool {
        let now_ms = std::time::SystemTime::now()
            .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)
            .unwrap_or_default()
            .as_millis();
        
        (now_ms - self.timestamp_ms) > MAX_QUOTE_AGE_MS
    }
    
    /// Check if quote is stale based on slot
    pub fn is_slot_stale(&self, current_slot: u64) -> bool {
        match self.slot {
            Some(quote_slot) => current_slot > quote_slot + MAX_SLOT_STALENESS,
            None => false, // If no slot info, rely on time-based staleness
        }
    }
    
    /// Get age in milliseconds
    pub fn age_ms(&self) -> u128 {
        let now_ms = std::time::SystemTime::now()
            .duration_since(std::time::UNIX_EPOCH)
            .unwrap_or_default()
            .as_millis();
        
        now_ms. saturating_sub(self.timestamp_ms)
    }
    
    /// Comprehensive freshness check
    pub fn is_fresh(&self, current_slot: Option<u64>) -> bool {
        if self.is_expired() {
            return false;
        }
        
        if let Some(slot) = current_slot {
            if self.is_slot_stale(slot) {
                return false;
            }
        }
        
        true
    }
}

/// Quote freshness validator
pub struct QuoteFreshnessValidator {
    pub max_age_ms: u128,
    pub max_slot_staleness: u64,
}

impl Default for QuoteFreshnessValidator {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            max_age_ms: MAX_QUOTE_AGE_MS,
            max_slot_staleness: MAX_SLOT_STALENESS,
        }
    }
}

impl QuoteFreshnessValidator {
    /// Validate a quote pair before execution
    pub async fn validate_quote_pair(
        &self,
        sell_quote: &TimestampedQuote,
        buy_quote: &TimestampedQuote,
        rpc: &AsyncRpcClient,
    ) -> Result<bool, String> {
        // Get current slot for slot-based validation
        let current_slot = match rpc.get_slot().await {
            Ok(slot) => Some(slot),
            Err(_) => None,
        };
        
        // Check sell quote freshness
        if !sell_quote.is_fresh(current_slot) {
            let age = sell_quote.age_ms();
            return Err(format!(
                "Sell quote from {} is stale (age: {}ms, max: {}ms)",
                sell_quote. dex_name, age, self.max_age_ms
            ));
        }
        
        // Check buy quote freshness
        if !buy_quote.is_fresh(current_slot) {
            let age = buy_quote. age_ms();
            return Err(format!(
                "Buy quote from {} is stale (age: {}ms, max: {}ms)",
                buy_quote. dex_name, age, self.max_age_ms
            ));
        }
        
        // Check combined age (both quotes should be obtained close together)
        let age_diff = if sell_quote.timestamp_ms > buy_quote.timestamp_ms {
            sell_quote.timestamp_ms - buy_quote.timestamp_ms
        } else {
            buy_quote.timestamp_ms - sell_quote.timestamp_ms
        };
        
        if age_diff > 1000 {
            // Quotes obtained more than 1 second apart
            return Err(format!(
                "Quote pair age difference too high: {}ms (quotes may not be comparable)",
                age_diff
            ));
        }
        
        Ok(true)
    }
    
    /// Pre-execution freshness check with re-fetch option
    pub async fn ensure_fresh_or_refetch<F, Fut>(
        &self,
        quote: &TimestampedQuote,
        current_slot: Option<u64>,
        refetch_fn: F,
    ) -> Result<TimestampedQuote, anyhow::Error>
    where
        F: FnOnce() -> Fut,
        Fut: std::future::Future<Output = Result<TimestampedQuote, anyhow::Error>>,
    {
        if quote. is_fresh(current_slot) {
            println!("   [FRESH] Quote from {} is fresh (age: {}ms)", 
                quote.dex_name, quote.age_ms());
            return Ok(quote.clone());
        }
        
        println!("   [STALE] Quote from {} is stale (age: {}ms), re-fetching...", 
            quote. dex_name, quote.age_ms());
        
        refetch_fn().await
    }
}

// ============================================================================
// --- DYNAMIC SLIPPAGE CALCULATION (FIX 2) ---
// ============================================================================

/// Configuration for dynamic slippage calculation
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
pub struct DynamicSlippageConfig {
    /// Minimum slippage in basis points (floor)
    pub min_slippage_bps: u32,
    /// Maximum slippage in basis points (ceiling)
    pub max_slippage_bps: u32,
    /// Base slippage for normal conditions
    pub base_slippage_bps: u32,
    /// Liquidity threshold below which we increase slippage (USD)
    pub low_liquidity_threshold_usd: f64,
    /// Liquidity threshold above which we can decrease slippage (USD)
    pub high_liquidity_threshold_usd: f64,
    /// Price impact threshold for additional slippage (percentage)
    pub price_impact_threshold_pct: f64,
    /// Volatility lookback period (number of price updates)
    pub volatility_window: usize,
}

impl Default for DynamicSlippageConfig {
    fn default() -> Self {
        Self {
            min_slippage_bps: 10,       // 0.1% minimum
            max_slippage_bps: 300,      // 3.0% maximum
            base_slippage_bps: 50,      // 0.5% default
            low_liquidity_threshold_usd: 50_000.0,
            high_liquidity_threshold_usd: 500_000.0,
            price_impact_threshold_pct: 0.5,
            volatility_window: 10,
        }
    }
}

/// Volatility tracker for dynamic slippage adjustment
struct VolatilityTracker {
    price_history: std::collections::VecDeque<(std::time::Instant, f64)>,
    max_history_size: usize,
}

impl VolatilityTracker {
    fn new(max_size: usize) -> Self {
        Self {
            price_history: std::collections::VecDeque::with_capacity(max_size),
            max_history_size: max_size,
        }
    }
    
    fn add_price(&mut self, price: f64) {
        let now = std::time::Instant::now();
        self.price_history.push_back((now, price));
        
        // Remove old entries
        while self.price_history.len() > self.max_history_size {
            self.price_history.pop_front();
        }
        
        // Also remove entries older than 5 minutes
        let cutoff = now - std::time::Duration::from_secs(300);
        while let Some((time, _)) = self.price_history.front() {
            if *time < cutoff {
                self.price_history.pop_front();
            } else {
                break;
            }
        }
    }
    
    /// Calculate volatility as percentage standard deviation
    fn calculate_volatility(&self) -> f64 {
        if self.price_history.len() < 2 {
            return 0.0;
        }
        
        let prices: Vec<f64> = self.price_history.iter().map(|(_, p)| *p).collect();
        let mean = prices.iter().sum::<f64>() / prices.len() as f64;
        
        if mean == 0.0 {
            return 0.0;
        }
        
        let variance = prices.iter()
            .map(|p| {
                let diff = (p - mean) / mean * 100.0; // Percentage diff
                diff * diff
            })
            .sum::<f64>() / prices.len() as f64;
        
        variance.sqrt()
    }
}

// Global volatility tracker
lazy_static::lazy_static! {
    static ref VOLATILITY_TRACKER: Arc<TokioRwLock<VolatilityTracker>> = 
        Arc::new(TokioRwLock::new(VolatilityTracker::new(50)));
    static ref DYNAMIC_SLIPPAGE_CONFIG: DynamicSlippageConfig = 
        DynamicSlippageConfig::default();
}

/// Calculate dynamic slippage based on pool liquidity, price impact, and market volatility
/// 
/// # Arguments
/// * `liquidity_usd` - Pool liquidity in USD
/// * `trade_amount_usd` - Trade size in USD
/// * `price_impact_pct` - Expected price impact percentage
/// * `current_price` - Current token price (for volatility tracking)
/// 
/// # Returns
/// Calculated slippage in basis points (bps)
pub async fn calculate_dynamic_slippage(
    liquidity_usd: Option<f64>,
    trade_amount_usd: f64,
    price_impact_pct: Option<f64>,
    current_price: Option<f64>,
) -> u32 {
    let config = &*DYNAMIC_SLIPPAGE_CONFIG;
    let mut slippage_bps = config.base_slippage_bps;
    
    // Update volatility tracker with current price
    if let Some(price) = current_price {
        let mut tracker = VOLATILITY_TRACKER.write().await;
        tracker.add_price(price);
    }
    
    // Get current volatility
    let volatility = {
        let tracker = VOLATILITY_TRACKER.read().await;
        tracker.calculate_volatility()
    };
    
    // =========================================================================
    // Factor 1: Liquidity-based adjustment
    // Lower liquidity = higher slippage needed
    // =========================================================================
    if let Some(liquidity) = liquidity_usd {
        if liquidity < config.low_liquidity_threshold_usd {
            // Low liquidity: increase slippage proportionally
            let liquidity_factor = (config.low_liquidity_threshold_usd / liquidity.max(1000.0)).min(3.0);
            let liquidity_adjustment = ((liquidity_factor - 1.0) * 50.0) as u32;
            slippage_bps += liquidity_adjustment;
            
            if liquidity_adjustment > 0 {
                println!("   [SLIPPAGE] Low liquidity adjustment: +{} bps (liq: ${:.0})", 
                    liquidity_adjustment, liquidity);
            }
        } else if liquidity > config.high_liquidity_threshold_usd {
            // High liquidity: can afford tighter slippage
            let reduction = ((liquidity / config.high_liquidity_threshold_usd).min(2.0) - 1.0) * 10.0;
            slippage_bps = slippage_bps.saturating_sub(reduction as u32);
            
            if reduction > 0.0 {
                println!("   [SLIPPAGE] High liquidity reduction: -{:.0} bps (liq: ${:.0})", 
                    reduction, liquidity);
            }
        }
    }
    
    // =========================================================================
    // Factor 2: Trade size relative to liquidity
    // Larger trades need more slippage protection
    // =========================================================================
    if let Some(liquidity) = liquidity_usd {
        if liquidity > 0.0 {
            let trade_ratio = trade_amount_usd / liquidity;
            
            if trade_ratio > 0.01 {
                // Trade is > 1% of pool liquidity
                let size_adjustment = ((trade_ratio * 100.0).min(10.0) * 10.0) as u32;
                slippage_bps += size_adjustment;
                
                println!("   [SLIPPAGE] Trade size adjustment: +{} bps (ratio: {:.2}%)", 
                    size_adjustment, trade_ratio * 100.0);
            }
        }
    }
    
    // =========================================================================
    // Factor 3: Price impact adjustment
    // Higher expected price impact = need more slippage buffer
    // =========================================================================
    if let Some(impact) = price_impact_pct {
        let impact_abs = impact.abs();
        
        if impact_abs > config.price_impact_threshold_pct {
            // Add slippage proportional to price impact above threshold
            let impact_excess = impact_abs - config.price_impact_threshold_pct;
            let impact_adjustment = (impact_excess * 50.0).min(100.0) as u32;
            slippage_bps += impact_adjustment;
            
            println!("   [SLIPPAGE] Price impact adjustment: +{} bps (impact: {:.2}%)", 
                impact_adjustment, impact_abs);
        }
    }
    
    // =========================================================================
    // Factor 4: Volatility adjustment
    // Higher market volatility = need more slippage
    // =========================================================================
    if volatility > 0.5 {
        // Volatility above 0.5% standard deviation
        let volatility_adjustment = ((volatility - 0.5) * 30.0).min(50.0) as u32;
        slippage_bps += volatility_adjustment;
        
        println!("   [SLIPPAGE] Volatility adjustment: +{} bps (vol: {:.2}%)", 
            volatility_adjustment, volatility);
    }
    
    // =========================================================================
    // Clamp to configured bounds
    // =========================================================================
    let final_slippage = slippage_bps.clamp(config.min_slippage_bps, config.max_slippage_bps);
    
    if final_slippage != slippage_bps {
        println!("   [SLIPPAGE] Clamped from {} to {} bps", slippage_bps, final_slippage);
    }
    
    final_slippage
}

/// Simplified slippage calculation for quick quotes
/// Uses conservative defaults when detailed data isn't available
pub fn calculate_quick_slippage(
    liquidity_usd: Option<f64>,
    trade_amount_usd: f64,
) -> u32 {
    let config = &*DYNAMIC_SLIPPAGE_CONFIG;
    let mut slippage_bps = config.base_slippage_bps;
    
    // Simple liquidity-based adjustment
    if let Some(liquidity) = liquidity_usd {
        if liquidity < 25_000.0 {
            slippage_bps = 150; // Very low liquidity
        } else if liquidity < 50_000.0 {
            slippage_bps = 100; // Low liquidity
        } else if liquidity < 100_000.0 {
            slippage_bps = 75;  // Medium-low liquidity
        } else if liquidity > 1_000_000.0 {
            slippage_bps = 30;  // High liquidity
        }
        
        // Additional adjustment for trade size
        let trade_ratio = trade_amount_usd / liquidity;
        if trade_ratio > 0.005 {
            slippage_bps += 25;
        }
        if trade_ratio > 0.01 {
            slippage_bps += 25;
        }
    }
    
    slippage_bps.clamp(config.min_slippage_bps, config.max_slippage_bps)
}

// ============================================================================
// --- TELEGRAM ALERTING ---
// ============================================================================

/// Send a Telegram alert message
async fn send_telegram_alert(message: &str) {
    if !TELEGRAM_ENABLED {
        return;
    }
    
    let bot_token = match std::env::var("TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN") {
        Ok(token) => token,
        Err(_) => {
            // Silently skip if not configured
            return;
        }
    };
    
    let chat_id = match std::env::var("TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID") {
        Ok(id) => id,
        Err(_) => {
            return;
        }
    };
    
    let url = format!("https://api.telegram.org/bot{}/sendMessage", bot_token);
    
    let client = reqwest::Client::new();
    let payload = json!({
        "chat_id": chat_id,
        "text": message,
        "parse_mode": "HTML"
    });
    
    match client.post(&url).json(&payload).send().await {
        Ok(resp) => {
            if !resp.status().is_success() {
                eprintln!("[Telegram] Failed to send alert: HTTP {}", resp.status());
            }
        }
        Err(e) => {
            eprintln!("[Telegram] Failed to send alert: {}", e);
        }
    }
}

/// Send opportunity alert
async fn alert_opportunity_found(
    sell_dex: &str,
    buy_dex: &str,
    spread_pct: f64,
    net_profit_usd: f64,
    confidence: f64,
    token_symbol: &str,
) {
    if net_profit_usd < TELEGRAM_MIN_PROFIT_ALERT {
        return;
    }
    
    let message = format!(
        " <b>Arbitrage Opportunity</b>\n\n\
         Spread: <b>{:.3}%</b>\n\
         Est. Profit: <b>${:.3}</b>\n\
         Confidence: <b>{:.1}%</b>\n\n\
         Sell: <b>{}</b>\n\
         Buy: <b>{}</b>\n\
         Token: <b>{}</b>\n\n\
         {}",
        spread_pct, net_profit_usd, confidence,
        sell_dex, buy_dex, token_symbol,
        chrono::Local::now().format("%H:%M:%S")
    );
    
    send_telegram_alert(&message).await;
}

/// Send trade execution alert
async fn alert_trade_executed(
    success: bool,
    actual_pnl: f64,
    tx1: &str,
    tx2: &str,
    token_symbol: &str,
) {
    let emoji = if success { "" } else { "" };
    let status = if success { "SUCCESS" } else { "FAILED" };
    
    let message = format!(
        "{} <b>Trade {}</b>\n\n\
         P&L: <b>${:.3}</b>\n\
         Token: {}\n\n\
         Tx1: <code>{}</code>\n\
         Tx2: <code>{}</code>\n\n\
         {}",
        emoji, status, actual_pnl, token_symbol,
        &tx1[..16.min(tx1.len())],
        &tx2[..16.min(tx2.len())],
        chrono::Local::now().format("%H:%M:%S")
    );
    
    send_telegram_alert(&message).await;
}

/// Send circuit breaker alert
async fn alert_circuit_breaker(reason: &str, until: &str) {
    let message = format!(
        " <b>CIRCUIT BREAKER ACTIVATED</b>\n\n\
         Reason: {}\n\
         Active until: {}\n\n\
        Bot trading is paused.",
        reason, until
    );
    
    send_telegram_alert(&message).await;
}

/// Send daily summary alert
async fn alert_daily_summary(
    daily_pnl: f64,
    trades_count: u32,
    success_rate: f64,
) {
    let emoji = if daily_pnl >= 0.0 { "" } else { "" };
    
    let message = format!(
        " <b>Daily Summary</b>\n\n\
        {} P&L: <b>${:.2}</b>\n\
         Trades: <b>{}</b>\n\
         Success Rate: <b>{:.1}%</b>\n\n\
         {}",
        emoji, daily_pnl, trades_count, success_rate,
        chrono::Local::now().format("%Y-%m-%d %H:%M")
    );
    
    send_telegram_alert(&message).await;
}

// ============================================================================
// --- PERSISTENT STATE ---
// ============================================================================

/// Persistent state that survives restarts
#[derive(Debug, Clone, Serialize, Deserialize)]
struct PersistentState {
    daily_pnl: f64,
    trades_today: u32,
    consecutive_failures: u32,
    last_reset_date: String,  // ISO date string
    total_profit_all_time: f64,
    total_trades_all_time: u32,
    successful_trades_all_time: u32,
    circuit_breaker_until: Option<String>,  // ISO datetime string
    last_saved: String,  // ISO datetime
}

impl PersistentState {
    fn new() -> Self {
        PersistentState {
            daily_pnl: 0.0,
            trades_today: 0,
            consecutive_failures: 0,
            last_reset_date: chrono::Local::now().format("%Y-%m-%d").to_string(),
            total_profit_all_time: 0.0,
            total_trades_all_time: 0,
            successful_trades_all_time: 0,
            circuit_breaker_until: None,
            last_saved: chrono::Local::now().to_rfc3339(),
        }
    }
    
    fn load() -> Self {
        match fs::read_to_string(STATE_FILE_PATH) {
            Ok(content) => {
                match serde_json::from_str(&content) {
                    Ok(state) => {
                        println!(" Loaded persistent state from {}", STATE_FILE_PATH);
                        state
                    }
                    Err(e) => {
                        eprintln!(" Failed to parse state file: {}, starting fresh", e);
                        PersistentState::new()
                    }
                }
            }
            Err(_) => {
                println!(" No existing state file, starting fresh");
                PersistentState::new()
            }
        }
    }
    
    fn save(&mut self) {
        self.last_saved = chrono::Local::now().to_rfc3339();
        
        match serde_json::to_string_pretty(self) {
            Ok(content) => {
                if let Err(e) = fs::write(STATE_FILE_PATH, content) {
                    eprintln!(" Failed to save state: {}", e);
                }
            }
            Err(e) => {
                eprintln!(" Failed to serialize state: {}", e);
            }
        }
    }
    
    fn check_daily_reset(&mut self) {
        let today = chrono::Local::now().format("%Y-%m-%d").to_string();
        if today != self.last_reset_date {
            // Send daily summary before resetting
            let success_rate = if self.trades_today > 0 {
                (self.successful_trades_all_time as f64 / self.total_trades_all_time as f64) * 100.0
            } else {
                0.0
            };
            
            // Spawn alert (don't await to avoid blocking)
            let pnl = self.daily_pnl;
            let trades = self.trades_today;
            tokio::spawn(async move {
                alert_daily_summary(pnl, trades, success_rate).await;
            });
            
            println!("\n Daily Reset - Previous day P&L: ${:.2}", self.daily_pnl);
            self.daily_pnl = 0.0;
            self.trades_today = 0;
            self.last_reset_date = today;
            self.save();
        }
    }
}

// ============================================================================
// --- ENHANCED WEBSOCKET STRUCTURES ---
// ============================================================================

/// Data source indicator for price updates
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
enum DataSource {
    WebSocket,
    API,
}

/// Enhanced price update with complete metadata
#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
struct EnhancedPriceUpdate {
    dex: String,
    token_pair: String,
    price: f64,
    timestamp: TokioInstant,
    liquidity: Option<f64>,
    data_source: DataSource,
    pool_address: String,
    reserve_token_a: Option<u64>,
    reserve_token_b: Option<u64>,
}

type EnhancedPriceCache = Arc<RwLock<HashMap<String, EnhancedPriceUpdate>>>;

fn create_enhanced_price_cache() -> EnhancedPriceCache {
    Arc::new(RwLock::new(HashMap::new()))
}

// ============================================================================
// --- PRICE CALCULATION FUNCTIONS ---
// ============================================================================

/// Calculate price from constant product AMM (x * y = k)
/// Returns price as quote_token / base_token
fn calculate_price_from_constant_product(
    reserve_a: u64,
    reserve_b: u64,
    decimals_a: u8,
    decimals_b: u8,
) -> f64 {
    if reserve_a == 0 {
        return 0.0;
    }
    
    let reserve_a_f64 = reserve_a as f64 / 10_f64.powi(decimals_a as i32);
    let reserve_b_f64 = reserve_b as f64 / 10_f64.powi(decimals_b as i32);
    reserve_b_f64 / reserve_a_f64
}

/// Calculate price from sqrt_price_x64 (used in CLMM/concentrated liquidity pools)
/// Formula: price = (sqrt_price / 2^64)^2
fn calculate_price_from_sqrt_price_x64(
    sqrt_price_x64_str: &str,
    decimals_a: u8,
    decimals_b: u8,
) -> Option<f64> {
    let sqrt_price_x64: u128 = sqrt_price_x64_str.parse().ok()?;
    let sqrt_price = sqrt_price_x64 as f64 / (1u128 << 64) as f64;
    let price = sqrt_price * sqrt_price;
    
    // Adjust for decimal differences
    let decimal_adjustment = 10_f64.powi((decimals_b as i32) - (decimals_a as i32));
    Some(price * decimal_adjustment)
}

/// Calculate total liquidity in USD
fn calculate_liquidity_usd(
    reserve_a: u64,
    reserve_b: u64,
    price_a_usd: f64,
    decimals_a: u8,
    decimals_b: u8,
) -> f64 {
    if reserve_a == 0 || reserve_b == 0 {
        return 0.0;
    }
    
    let reserve_a_f64 = reserve_a as f64 / 10_f64.powi(decimals_a as i32);
    let reserve_b_f64 = reserve_b as f64 / 10_f64.powi(decimals_b as i32);
    
    let value_a_usd = reserve_a_f64 * price_a_usd;
    let price = reserve_b_f64 / reserve_a_f64;
    let price_b_usd = price_a_usd * price;
    let value_b_usd = reserve_b_f64 * price_b_usd;
    
    value_a_usd + value_b_usd
}

/// Connect to WebSocket and monitor pool account updates (FIXED VERSION WITH DIAGNOSTICS)
async fn connect_and_monitor_pools_shared(
    subscriptions: Vec<(String, String)>,
    price_cache: EnhancedPriceCache,
    token_a_mint: &str,
    token_b_mint: &str,
) -> anyhow::Result<()> {
    let rpc = AsyncRpcClient::new_with_commitment(
        QUICKNODE_RPC_URL.to_string(),
        CommitmentConfig::confirmed(),
    );
    
    if WS_DEBUG_MODE {
        println!("[WS] Connecting to WebSocket endpoint...");
    }
    
    let (ws_stream, response) = connect_async(QUICKNODE_WS_URL).await?;
    let (mut write, mut read) = ws_stream.split();
    
    let mut request_id_to_pool: HashMap<u64, (String, String)> = HashMap::new();
    let mut sub_id_to_pool: HashMap<u64, (String, String)> = HashMap::new();
    
    println!(" Single WebSocket connection established");
    println!(" Subscribing to {} pools...\n", subscriptions.len());
    
    // Test subscription: slotSubscribe to verify WebSocket is receiving data
    let slot_test_msg = json!({
        "jsonrpc": "2.0",
        "id": 9999,
        "method": "slotSubscribe"
    });
    write.send(Message::Text(slot_test_msg.to_string())).await?;
    if WS_DEBUG_MODE {
        println!("[WS] [DIAG] Sent slotSubscribe test (id: 9999)");
    }
    
    // Send account subscriptions
    for (idx, (dex_name, pool_address)) in subscriptions.iter().enumerate() {
        let request_id = (idx + 1) as u64;
        
        let subscribe_msg = json!({
            "jsonrpc": "2.0",
            "id": request_id,
            "method": "accountSubscribe",
            "params": [
                pool_address,
                {
                    "encoding": "base64",
                    "commitment": "confirmed"
                }
            ]
        });
        
        write.send(Message::Text(subscribe_msg.to_string())).await?;
        println!("   [{}] Subscribed to pool {}... (id: {})", dex_name, &pool_address[..12], request_id);
        
        request_id_to_pool.insert(request_id, (dex_name.clone(), pool_address.clone()));
        tokio::time::sleep(Duration::from_millis(100)).await;
    }
    
    println!("\n All {} subscriptions sent on single connection", subscriptions.len());
    
    let mut ping_interval = tokio::time::interval(Duration::from_secs(WS_HEARTBEAT_INTERVAL_SECS));
    let mut last_any_message = TokioInstant::now();
    let mut last_data_update = TokioInstant::now();
    let mut message_count = 0u64;
    let mut notification_count = 0u64;
    let mut confirmed_subscriptions = 0usize;
    let mut slot_updates = 0u64;
    
    loop {
        tokio::select! {
            _ = ping_interval.tick() => {
                if write.send(Message::Ping(vec![])).await.is_err() {
                    println!(" Ping failed, reconnecting...");
                    break;
                }
                
                let since_any = last_any_message.elapsed().as_secs();
                let since_data = last_data_update.elapsed().as_secs();
                
                let cache = price_cache.read().await;
                let active_prices = cache.len();
                drop(cache);
                
                // Enhanced heartbeat
                println!(" Heartbeat | Subs: {}/{} | Msgs: {} | Notifs: {} | Slots: {} | Cache: {} | Age: {}s", 
                    confirmed_subscriptions, subscriptions.len(),
                    message_count, notification_count, slot_updates, active_prices,
                    since_data);
                
                // Diagnostic warning
                if slot_updates > 5 && notification_count == 0 && confirmed_subscriptions > 0 {
                    println!(" [DIAG] âš  Slots arriving but 0 account notifications - likely no trades on pools");
                }
                
                if since_any > 30 {
                    println!(" No messages for {}s, reconnecting...", since_any);
                    break;
                }
                
                if since_data > WS_STALE_TIMEOUT_SECS {
                    println!(" No updates for {}s, reconnecting...", WS_STALE_TIMEOUT_SECS);
                    break;
                }
            }
            
            msg = read.next() => {
                match msg {
                    Some(Ok(Message::Text(text))) => {
                        message_count += 1;
                        last_any_message = TokioInstant::now();
                        
                        if let Ok(data) = serde_json::from_str::<serde_json::Value>(&text) {
                            // Handle subscription confirmations
                            if let Some(result) = data.get("result") {
                                if let Some(request_id) = data.get("id").and_then(|i| i.as_u64()) {
                                    // Slot test confirmation
                                    if request_id == 9999 {
                                        if WS_DEBUG_MODE {
                                            println!("[WS] [DIAG] âœ“ slotSubscribe confirmed - WebSocket functional");
                                        }
                                        continue;
                                    }
                                    
                                    // Account subscription confirmation
                                    if let Some(sub_id) = result.as_u64() {
                                        if let Some((dex_name, pool_address)) = request_id_to_pool.get(&request_id) {
                                            sub_id_to_pool.insert(sub_id, (dex_name.clone(), pool_address.clone()));
                                            confirmed_subscriptions += 1;
                                            println!("    [{}] Subscription confirmed (request_id: {} -> sub_id: {})", 
                                                dex_name, request_id, sub_id);
                                            println!("    [{}] Mapped: sub_id {} -> pool {}...", 
                                                dex_name, sub_id, &pool_address[..12]);
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                continue;
                            }
                            
                            // Handle slot notifications (diagnostic)
                            if data.get("method").and_then(|m| m.as_str()) == Some("slotNotification") {
                                slot_updates += 1;
                                if WS_DEBUG_MODE && slot_updates <= 2 {
                                    println!("[WS] [DIAG] Slot notification #{} - WebSocket receiving data", slot_updates);
                                }
                                continue;
                            }
                            
                            // Handle account notifications (THE IMPORTANT ONES)
                            if data.get("method").and_then(|m| m.as_str()) == Some("accountNotification") {
                                notification_count += 1;
                                last_data_update = TokioInstant::now();
                                
                                println!("[WS] â˜… accountNotification #{} received!", notification_count);
                                
                                if let Some(params) = data.get("params") {
                                    if let Some(sub_id) = params.get("subscription").and_then(|s| s.as_u64()) {
                                        if let Some((dex_name, pool_address)) = sub_id_to_pool.get(&sub_id) {
                                            println!("[WS]   â†’ {} (pool: {}...)", dex_name, &pool_address[..12]);
                                            
                                            if let Some(price_update) = parse_account_update_shared(
                                                &data, 
                                                dex_name, 
                                                pool_address, 
                                                price_cache.clone(),
                                                token_a_mint,
                                                token_b_mint,
                                                &rpc,
                                            ).await {
                                                let pool_prefix = &pool_address[..8.min(pool_address.len())];
                                                let key = format!("{}-{}", dex_name, pool_prefix);
                                                println!("[WS]   âœ“ Price: ${:.6} -> {}", price_update.price, key);
                                                price_cache.write().await.insert(key, price_update);
                                            }
                                        } else {
                                            println!("[WS]   âš  Unknown sub_id: {}", sub_id);
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                continue;
                            }
                            
                            // Handle errors
                            if let Some(error) = data.get("error") {
                                println!("[WS] [ERROR] {:?}", error);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                    Some(Ok(Message::Pong(_))) => {
                        last_any_message = TokioInstant::now();
                    }
                    Some(Ok(Message::Ping(data))) => {
                        last_any_message = TokioInstant::now();
                        let _ = write.send(Message::Pong(data)).await;
                    }
                    Some(Ok(Message::Close(reason))) => {
                        println!(" WebSocket closed: {:?}", reason);
                        break;
                    }
                    None => {
                        println!(" WebSocket stream ended");
                        break;
                    }
                    Some(Err(e)) => {
                        eprintln!(" WebSocket error: {}", e);
                        break;
                    }
                    _ => {}
                }
            }
        }
    }
    
    println!(" Connection stats: Messages: {}, Notifications: {}, Slots: {}, Confirmed: {}/{}", 
        message_count, notification_count, slot_updates, confirmed_subscriptions, subscriptions.len());
    Ok(())
}

// ============================================================================
// --- PRICE DIRECTION CORRECTION ---
// ============================================================================

/// Correct price direction using Jupiter reference price
/// This handles cases where pools store tokens in different orders (A/B vs B/A)
/// Returns the corrected price (either original or inverted)
/// Correct price direction using Jupiter reference price
/// Returns None if the price is more than 50% off expected (likely bad data)
async fn correct_price_direction(
    raw_price: f64,
    dex_name: &str,
    base_token_mint: &str,
    quote_token_mint: &str,
) -> Option<f64> {
    // Skip correction for SOL/USDC pairs (usually correct)
    if (base_token_mint == SOL_MINT && quote_token_mint == USDC_MINT) ||
       (base_token_mint == USDC_MINT && quote_token_mint == SOL_MINT) {
        return Some(raw_price);
    }
    
    // Get Jupiter prices for both tokens to calculate expected ratio
    let base_usd_price = get_jupiter_token_price(base_token_mint).await;
    let quote_usd_price = get_jupiter_token_price(quote_token_mint).await;
    
    if base_usd_price <= 0.0 || quote_usd_price <= 0.0 {
        println!("[{}] [PRICE_CORRECT] Cannot get Jupiter prices, using raw price", dex_name);
        return Some(raw_price);
    }
    
    // Expected price = base_usd / quote_usd
    let expected_price = base_usd_price / quote_usd_price;
    let reciprocal_price = if raw_price > 0.0 { 1.0 / raw_price } else { 0.0 };
    
    // Calculate deviations
    let raw_deviation = if expected_price > 0.0 {
        ((raw_price - expected_price) / expected_price).abs()
    } else {
        f64::MAX
    };
    
    let reciprocal_deviation = if expected_price > 0.0 {
        ((reciprocal_price - expected_price) / expected_price).abs()
    } else {
        f64::MAX
    };
    
    println!("[{}] [PRICE_CORRECT] Raw: {:.8}, Reciprocal: {:.8}, Expected: {:.8}", 
        dex_name, raw_price, reciprocal_price, expected_price);
    println!("[{}] [PRICE_CORRECT] Raw deviation: {:.2}%, Reciprocal deviation: {:.2}%", 
        dex_name, raw_deviation * 100.0, reciprocal_deviation * 100.0);
    
    // Determine the best price and its deviation
    let (best_price, best_deviation, direction) = if reciprocal_deviation < raw_deviation {
        (reciprocal_price, reciprocal_deviation, "RECIPROCAL")
    } else {
        (raw_price, raw_deviation, "RAW")
    };
    
    // =========================================================================
    // IMPROVED THRESHOLD LOGIC (FIX 3)
    // =========================================================================
    // Different pools can have different reserve ratios due to:
    //   - Arbitrage lag between pools
    //   - Different fee structures  
    //   - Price impact from recent large trades
    //
    // Tiered acceptance:
    //   - < 25% deviation: HIGH confidence
    //   - 25-50% deviation: MEDIUM confidence
    //   - 50-75% deviation: LOW confidence (still accept)
    //   - > 75% deviation: REJECT
    // =========================================================================
    
    const HIGH_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD: f64 = 0.25;   // 25%
    const MEDIUM_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD: f64 = 0.50; // 50%
    const LOW_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD: f64 = 0.75;    // 75% (INCREASED from 50%)
    
    if best_deviation <= HIGH_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD {
        println!("[{}] [PRICE_CORRECT] HIGH CONFIDENCE: Using {} price ({:.1}% deviation)", 
            dex_name, direction, best_deviation * 100.0);
        return Some(best_price);
    }
    
    if best_deviation <= MEDIUM_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD {
        println!("[{}] [PRICE_CORRECT] MEDIUM CONFIDENCE: Using {} price ({:.1}% deviation)", 
            dex_name, direction, best_deviation * 100.0);
        return Some(best_price);
    }
    
    if best_deviation <= LOW_CONFIDENCE_THRESHOLD {
        // Check if one direction is significantly better than the other
        let direction_ratio = if raw_deviation > 0.0 && reciprocal_deviation > 0.0 {
            (raw_deviation / reciprocal_deviation).max(reciprocal_deviation / raw_deviation)
        } else {
            1.0
        };
        
        // If one direction is at least 10x better, use it with confidence
        if direction_ratio >= 10.0 {
            println!("[{}] [PRICE_CORRECT] LOW CONFIDENCE (clear direction): Using {} price ({:.1}% deviation)", 
                dex_name, direction, best_deviation * 100.0);
            return Some(best_price);
        }
        
        // Otherwise, still accept but with warning
        println!("[{}] [PRICE_CORRECT] LOW CONFIDENCE: Accepting {} price ({:.1}% deviation)", 
            dex_name, direction, best_deviation * 100.0);
        println!("[{}] [PRICE_CORRECT] Note: Reserve ratio may differ from market price", dex_name);
        return Some(best_price);
    }
    
    // > 75% deviation - reject
    println!("[{}] [PRICE_CORRECT] REJECTED: Best price {:.8} is {:.1}% off expected {:.8}", 
        dex_name, best_price, best_deviation * 100.0, expected_price);
    println!("[{}] [PRICE_CORRECT] This pool likely has wrong token order or stale reserves", dex_name);
    None
}

/// Get token price from Jupiter API
async fn get_jupiter_token_price(mint: &str) -> f64 {
    // Handle known tokens with special mints
    if mint == SOL_MINT {
        // Fetch SOL price
        if let Ok(info) = search_token_by_address(mint).await {
            if let Some(price) = info.usd_price {
                return price;
            }
        }
        return 0.0;
    }
    
    // For other tokens, use Jupiter API
    match search_token_by_address(mint).await {
        Ok(info) => info.usd_price.unwrap_or(0.0),
        Err(_) => 0.0,
    }
}


/// Parse account update for shared WebSocket - WITH VALIDATION

async fn parse_account_update_shared(
    data: &serde_json::Value,
    dex_name: &str,
    pool_address: &str,
    price_cache: EnhancedPriceCache,  //  Add this parameter
    token_a_mint: &str, // NEW PARAMETER
    token_b_mint: &str, // NEW PARAMETER
    rpc: &AsyncRpcClient, // NEW PARAMETER
) -> Option<EnhancedPriceUpdate> {
    let params = data.get("params")?;
    let result = params.get("result")? ;
